Store-level sales with proper modeling\nstore_sales = sales_all.groupby('store_id')['revenue'].sum().reset_index()\nstore_traffic = traffic_all.groupby('store_id')['customer_count'].sum().reset_index()\nstore_data = stores.merge(store_sales, on='store_id').merge(store_traffic, on='store_id')\n\n# Simple metric: revenue per store_size_sqm normalized by region\nfor region, grp in store_data.groupby('region'):\n    mean = grp['total_revenue'].mean()\n    std = grp['total_revenue'].std()\n    store_data.loc[grp.index, 'revenue_region_z'] = (grp['total_revenue'] - mean) / std if std > 0 else 0\n    \n    mean_ps = grp['total_revenue'].div(grp['store_size_sqm']).mean()\n    std_ps = grp['total_revenue'].div(grp['store_size_sqm']).std()\n    store_data.loc[grp.index, 'revenue_per_sqm_region_z'] = (grp['total_revenue'].div(grp['store_size_sqm']) - mean_ps) / std_ps if std_ps > 0 else 0\n\n# 2. 'checkout', 'pos_materials', 'eye_level', 'visit_count', 'avg_duration']\n    \n    # Combined z-score\n    all_metrics = sale_metrics + qual_metrics\n    \n    z_df = pd.DataFrame({'rep_id': group['rep_id']})\n    for m in all_metrics:\n        if group[m].std() > 1e-10:\n            z_df[m + '_z'] = (group[m] - group[m].mean()) / group[m].std()\n    \n    # Sales composite (only sales metrics)\n    sale_z_cols = [c for c in z_df.columns if c.startswith('avg_rev')]\n    z_df['sales_composite'] = z_df[sale_z_cols].mean(axis=1) if sale_z_cols else 0\n    \n    # Quality composite (only quality metrics)\n    qual_z_cols = [c for c in z_df.columns if any(q in c for q in ['compliance_z', 'facings_z', 'endcap_z', 'checkout_z', 'pos_materials_z', 'eye_level_z', 'visit_count_z', for i in range(1, 13)], ignore_index=True)\nshelf_audits = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/shelf_audit_{str(i).zfill(3)}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)], ignore_index=True)\n\n# Aggregate\nss =
